### <a id="the-inductive-types-h-s-p-v">The Inductive Types H, S, P, V</a>

This section presents the [Varieties.Varieties][] module of the [Agda Universal Algebra Library][].

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="329" class="Symbol">{-#</a> <a id="333" class="Keyword">OPTIONS</a> <a id="341" class="Pragma">--without-K</a> <a id="353" class="Pragma">--exact-split</a> <a id="367" class="Pragma">--safe</a> <a id="374" class="Symbol">#-}</a>

<a id="379" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="384" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="391" href="Algebras.Signatures.html" class="Module">Algebras.Signatures</a> <a id="411" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="418" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a><a id="427" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="429" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5600" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a><a id="430" class="Symbol">;</a> <a id="432" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="433" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="435" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="440" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="447" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html" class="Module">MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems</a> <a id="473" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="479" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="480" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="494" class="Symbol">)</a>


<a id="498" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="505" href="Varieties.Varieties.html" class="Module">Varieties.Varieties</a> <a id="525" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="526" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a> <a id="528" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="530" href="Algebras.Signatures.html#1299" class="Function">Signature</a> <a id="540" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#5600" class="Generalizable">𝓞</a> <a id="542" href="Universes.html#262" class="Generalizable">𝓥</a><a id="543" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="545" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#545" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="549" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="551" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html#3468" class="Function">global-dfunext</a><a id="565" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="567" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="574" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="579" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="586" href="Varieties.EquationalLogic.html" class="Module">Varieties.EquationalLogic</a><a id="611" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="612" class="Argument">𝑆</a> <a id="614" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="616" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="617" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="619" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#545" class="Bound">gfe</a><a id="622" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="624" class="Keyword">public</a>
<a id="631" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="636" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="643" href="MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems.html" class="Module">MGS-Subsingleton-Theorems</a> <a id="669" class="Keyword">using</a> <a id="675" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="676" href="MGS-FunExt-from-Univalence.html#2235" class="Function">hfunext</a><a id="683" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="685" class="Comment">-- public</a>

</pre>


Fix a signature 𝑆, let 𝒦 be a class of 𝑆-algebras, and define

* H 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a homomorphic image of a members of 𝒦;
* S 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a subalgebra of a member of 𝒦;
* P 𝒦 = algebras isomorphic to a product of members of 𝒦.

A straight-forward verification confirms that H, S, and P are **closure operators** (expansive, monotone, and idempotent).  A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is said to be *closed under the taking of homomorphic images* provided `H 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`. Similarly, 𝒦 is *closed under the taking of subalgebras* (resp., *arbitrary products*) provided `S 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦` (resp., `P 𝒦 ⊆ 𝒦`). The operators H, S, and P can be composed with one another repeatedly, forming yet more closure operators.

An algebra is a homomorphic image (resp., subalgebra; resp., product) of every algebra to which it is isomorphic. Thus, the class `H 𝒦` (resp., `S 𝒦`; resp., `P 𝒦`) is closed under isomorphism.

A **variety** is a class of algebras, in the same signature, that is closed under the taking of homomorphic images, subalgebras, and arbitrary products.  To represent varieties we define inductive types for the closure operators `H`, `S`, and `P` that are composable.  Separately, we define an inductive type `V` which simultaneously represents closure under all three operators, `H`, `S`, and `P`.




#### <a id="homomorphic-closure">Homomorphic closure</a>

We define the inductive type `H` to represent classes of algebras that include all homomorphic images of algebras in the class; i.e., classes that are closed under the taking of homomorphic images.

#### <a id="subalgebraic-closure">Subalgebraic closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of a class of algebras that is closed under the taking of subalgebras is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="2934" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="S"></a><a id="2939" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="2941" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="2942" id="2989" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="2993" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="2994" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a><a id="3001" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3002" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2942" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3004" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3006" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3007" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="3008" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3009" class="Symbol">)(</a><a  <a id="S.ssubw"></a><a id="3228" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3228" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="3234" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3236" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3237" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3237" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3239" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3239" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3241" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="3243" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="3251" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="3253" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="3254" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3256" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3258" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3237" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3260" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3262" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="3263" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3264" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2942" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="3265" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="3267" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2944" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="3268" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="3270" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2958" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="3272" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3274" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3239" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3276" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#3954" class="Function Operator">≤</a> <a id="3278" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3237" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="3280" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="3282" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3239" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="3284" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="3286" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="3288" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2958" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="product-closure">Product closure</a>

The most useful inductive type that we have found for representing the semantic notion of an class of algebras closed under the taking of arbitrary products is the following.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="3623" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="P"></a><a id="3628" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="3630" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="3631" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="3691" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3631" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="3693" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="3695" id="4075" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4077" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4079" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="P.pisou"></a><a id="4082" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4082" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a>  <a id="4089" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4091" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4092" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4092" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4094" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4096" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4104" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3631" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4106" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4107" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4109" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4109" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4111" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4113" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4121" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4123" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4124" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4126" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4128" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4092" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4130" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4132" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4133" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4134" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3631" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4135" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4137" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3631" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4138" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4140" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4142" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4144" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4092" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4146" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4148" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4109" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4150" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4152" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4109" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4154" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4156" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4158" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="P.pisow"></a><a id="4161" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4161" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a>  <a id="4168" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4170" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4171" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4171" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4173" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4173" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4175" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4177" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4185" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="4187" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4188" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4190" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4192" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4171" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4194" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4196" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="4197" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4198" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3631" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="4199" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="4201" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3633" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="4202" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="4204" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4206" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4208" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4171" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="4210" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="4212" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4173" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4214" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="4216" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4173" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="4218" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="4220" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="4222" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3647" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="varietal-closure">Varietal closure</a>

A class 𝒦 of 𝑆-algebras is called a **variety** if it is closed under each of the closure operators H, S, and P introduced above; the corresponding closure operator is often denoted 𝕍, but we will denote it by `V`.

We now define `V` as an inductive type.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="4562" class="Keyword">data</a> <a id="V"></a><a id="4567" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="4569" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="4570" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4570" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4572" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4572" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="4574" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4576" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="4584" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="4586" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="4588" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4590" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="4594" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4595" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="4603" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4570" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4605" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="4606" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="4608" id="4617" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="4621" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4622" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a><a id="4629" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4630" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4570" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="4632" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="4634" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="5170" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5172" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5172" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5174" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5176" <a id="5190" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5191" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5193" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5195" class="Symbol">(∀</a> <a id="5198" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5198" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="5200" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5202" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5203" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5172" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5198" class="Bound">i</a><a id="5206" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5208" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5210" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5211" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5212" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4570" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5213" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5215" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4572" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5216" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5218" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="5219" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5221" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5223" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="5225" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5172" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="5227" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5229" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5231" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visou"></a><a id="5234" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5234" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a>  <a id="5241" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5243" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5244" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5244" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5246" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5248" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5256" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4570" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5258" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5259" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5261" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5261" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5263" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5265" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5273" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5275" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5276" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5278" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5280" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5244" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5282" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5284" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5285" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5286" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4570" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5287" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5289" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4570" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5290" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5292" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5294" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5296" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5244" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5298" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5300" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5261" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5302" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5304" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5261" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5306" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5308" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5310" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="V.visow"></a><a id="5313" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5313" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a>  <a id="5320" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5322" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5323" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5323" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5325" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5325" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5327" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5329" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5337" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="5339" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5340" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5342" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5344" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5323" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5346" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5348" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5349" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5350" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4570" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5351" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5353" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4572" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="5354" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5356" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="5358" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5360" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5323" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="5362" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="5364" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5325" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5366" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5368" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5325" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="5370" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="5372" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="5374" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4586" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

</pre>

Thus, if 𝒦 is a class of 𝑆-algebras, then the **variety generated by** 𝒦 is denoted by `V 𝒦` and defined to be the smallest class that contains 𝒦 and is closed under `H`, `S`, and `P`.

With the closure operator V representing closure under HSP, we represent formally what it means to be a variety of algebras as follows.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="is-variety"></a><a id="5726" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5726" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5737" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5739" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5740" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5740" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5742" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5744" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5752" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="5754" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5754" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5756" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5758" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5763" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5764" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5772" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5740" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5774" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5775" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5777" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5780" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5740" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5781" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5784" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5786" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5789" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5740" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5791" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5793" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5726" class="Function">is-variety</a><a id="5803" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5804" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5804" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5805" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5807" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5807" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5809" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5811" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="5812" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5804" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5814" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="5816" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5804" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5817" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5819" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5807" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5821" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="5823" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5807" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

<a id="variety"></a><a id="5826" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5826" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5834" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5836" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5837" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5837" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5839" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5841" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="5849" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5851" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5853" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5854" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5857" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5837" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5858" class="Symbol">)</a><a id="5859" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a> <a id="5861" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a>
<a id="5863" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5826" class="Function">variety</a> <a id="5871" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5871" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5873" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="5875" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">Σ</a> <a id="5877" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5877" class="Bound">𝒱</a> <a id="5879" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">꞉</a> <a id="5881" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5882" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="5887" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5888" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="5896" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5871" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="5898" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="5899" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="5901" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="5904" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5871" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="5905" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="5908" href="MGS-MLTT.html#3074" class="Function">,</a> <a id="5910" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5726" class="Function">is-variety</a> <a id="5921" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5877" class="Bound">𝒱</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="V-is-closed-under-lift">V is closed under lift</a>

As mentioned earlier, a technical hurdle that must be overcome when formalizing proofs in Agda is the proper handling of universe levels. In particular, in the proof of the Birkhoff's theorem, for example, we will need to know that if an algebra 𝑨 belongs to the variety V 𝒦, then so does the lift of 𝑨.  Let us get the tedious proof of this technical lemma out of the way.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="6390" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="6395" href="Prelude.Lifts.html#2741" class="Module">Lift</a>
<a id="6400" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="6407" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6407" class="Module">_</a> <a id="6409" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6410" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6412" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6414" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="6422" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6424" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6424" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="6426" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6428" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="6433" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6434" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6442" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6444" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6445" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="6447" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6450" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6451" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="6454" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="6462" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6462" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6466" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6468" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6469" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6469" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6471" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6473" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="6481" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6482" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6485" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6486" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6488" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="6489" class="Symbol">}</a>
  <a id="6493" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="6498" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6469" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6500" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6502" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6503" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6504" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6505" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6507" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6510" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6511" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6513" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6424" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
       <a id="6522" class="Comment">--------------------------------------</a>
  <a id="6563" class="Symbol">→</a>    <a id="6568" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="6577" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6469" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="6579" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6580" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6583" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6585" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6586" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6588" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="6590" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="6591" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="6593" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="6595" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="6598" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6410" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="6600" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="6601" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6603" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6424" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="6607" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6462" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="6611" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6612" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4658" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a><a id="6617" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="6618" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6618" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6619" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="6621" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6621" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6622" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6624" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="6626" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5313" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="6632" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6633" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4658" class="InductiveConstructor">vbase</a> <a id="6639" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6621" class="Bound">x</a><a id="6640" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6643" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6514" class="Function">lift-alg-associative</a> <a id="6664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6618" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="6665" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="7762" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">iso-components</a> <a id="7777" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7779" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7780" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7780" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7782" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7784" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7462" class="Bound">I</a><a id="7785" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7787" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="7789" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7465" class="Bound">𝒜</a> <a id="7791" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7780" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7793" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="7795" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7619" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="7798" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7799" href="Prelude.Lifts.html#2803" class="InductiveConstructor">lift</a> <a id="7804" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7780" class="Bound">i</a><a id="7805" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="7809" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">iso-components</a> <a id="7824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7824" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="7826" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7828" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4959" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a>

  <a id="7842" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7842" class="Function">B≅A</a> <a id="7846" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="7848" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7559" class="Function">lA+</a> <a id="7852" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="7854" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="7856" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7619" class="Function">lA</a>
  <a id="7861" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7842" class="Function">B≅A</a> <a id="7865" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7867" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#7998" class="Function">lift-alg-⨅≅</a> <a id="7879" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#545" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="7883" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7762" class="Function">iso-components</a>

 <a id="7900" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6462" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7904" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7905" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5234" class="InductiveConstructor">visou</a><a id="7910" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7911" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7911" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7912" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7914" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7914" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7915" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7917" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7917" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7919" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7919" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7922" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7924" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7926" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5313" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7932" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7933" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4715" class="InductiveConstructor">vlift</a> <a id="7939" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7917" class="Bound">x</a><a id="7940" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7942" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7943" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5809" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="7956" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7919" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7959" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="7962" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6462" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7966" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7967" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5313" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a><a id="7972" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="7973" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7973" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="7974" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="7976" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7976" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="7977" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="7979" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7979" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="7981" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7981" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="7984" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="7986" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="7988" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5313" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="7994" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="7995" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#6462" class="Function">VlA</a> <a id="7999" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7979" class="Bound">x</a><a id="8000" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8002" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8003" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#5809" class="Function">lift-alg-iso</a> <a id="8016" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#7981" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="8019" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="closure-properties">Closure properties</a>

The types defined above represent operators with useful closure properties. We now prove a handful of such properties that we need later.

First, `P` is a closure operator.  This is proved by checking that `P` is *monotone*, *expansive*, and *idempotent*. The meaning of these terms will be clear from the definitions of the types that follow.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P-mono"></a><a id="8451" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8451" class="Function">P-mono</a> <a id="8458" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8460" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="8461" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8461" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8463" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8463" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="8465" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8467" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="8475" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="8477" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8477" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="8479" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8479" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="8482" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8484" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a><a id="8488" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8489" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="8497" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8461" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="8499" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="8500" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="8502" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="8505" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8461" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="8506" class="Symbol">)}</a>

  <a id="9137" class="Symbol">→</a>        <a id="9146" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="9147" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9148" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9070" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9150" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9152" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9072" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9153" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9155" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9070" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9157" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9159" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9072" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9160" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9162" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9163" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="9164" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9165" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9070" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9166" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9168" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9070" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9170" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9172" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9072" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9173" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9175" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9105" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="9176" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9178" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9180" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="9181" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9182" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9070" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9183" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9185" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9070" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9187" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="9189" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9072" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9190" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9192" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9105" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="9196" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9094" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9204" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9205" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3719" class="InductiveConstructor">pbase</a> <a id="9211" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9211" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9212" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9217" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9219" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3841" class="InductiveConstructor">pliftw</a> <a id="9226" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9211" class="Bound">x</a>

 <a id="9315" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9094" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9323" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9324" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3918" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="9330" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9330" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9331" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9336" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9338" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4000" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9344" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9347" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9347" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9349" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9351" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9094" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9359" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9360" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9330" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9362" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9347" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9363" class="Symbol">))</a>
 <a id="9367" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9094" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9375" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9376" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4000" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9382" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9382" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9383" class="Symbol">)</a>    <a id="9388" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9390" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4000" class="InductiveConstructor">prodw</a> <a id="9396" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9399" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9399" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="9401" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9403" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9094" class="Function">P-idemp</a> <a id="9411" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9412" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9382" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9414" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9399" class="Bound">i</a><a id="9415" class="Symbol">))</a>

</pre>

Similarly, S is a closure operator.  The facts that S is idempotent and expansive won't be needed below, so we omit these, but we will make use of monotonicity of S.  Here is the proof of the latter.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="S-mono"></a><a id="9736" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9736" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9743" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9745" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9746" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9746" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9748" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9748" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="9750" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9752" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="9760" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9762" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9762" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9764" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9764" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9767" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9769" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="9774" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9775" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="9783" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9746" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="9785" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="9786" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="9788" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="9791" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9746" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9792" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="9796" class="Symbol">→</a>       <a id="9804" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9762" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9806" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9808" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9764" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a> <a id="9811" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9814" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9815" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9746" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9816" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9818" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9748" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9819" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9821" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9762" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="9823" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="9825" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="9826" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9827" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9746" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="9828" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="9830" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9748" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="9831" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9833" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9764" class="Bound">𝒦&#39;</a>

<a id="9837" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9736" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9844" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9844" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9848" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9849" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3030" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9855" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9855" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9856" class="Symbol">)</a>            <a id="9869" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9871" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3030" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a> <a id="9877" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9878" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9844" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9882" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9855" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9883" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="9885" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9736" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9892" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9892" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9896" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9897" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3086" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="9902" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="9903" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9903" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="9904" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="9906" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9906" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9907" class="Symbol">)</a>         <a id="9917" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9919" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3086" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a> <a id="9925" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9926" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9736" class="Function">S-mono</a> <a id="9933" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9892" class="Bound">kk&#39;</a> <a id="9937" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#9906" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9938" class="Symbol">)</a>

</pre>

We sometimes want to go back and forth between our two representations of subalgebras of algebras in a class. The tools `subalgebra→S` and `S→subalgebra` are made for that purpose.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="10325" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10332" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10332" class="Module">_</a> <a id="10334" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10335" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10335" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10337" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10337" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="10339" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10341" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="10349" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10351" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10351" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10353" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10355" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="10360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10361" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10369" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10335" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10371" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10372" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="10374" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="10377" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10335" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10378" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="10381" class="Keyword">where</a>

 <a id="10389" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10389" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10402" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10404" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10405" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10405" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10407" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="10409" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="10417" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10418" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10335" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="10420" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="10422" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10337" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10423" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10425" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="10426" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10428" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10430" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10405" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10432" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#4183" class="Function Operator">IsSubalgebraOfClass</a> <a id="10452" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10351" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="10454" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="10456" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10405" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="10458" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="10460" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="10461" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10462" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10335" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="10463" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="10465" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10337" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="10466" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10468" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10351" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

 <a id="10472" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10389" class="Function">subalgebra→S</a> <a id="10485" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="10486" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10486" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="10487" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="10489" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="10490" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10490" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="10492" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10494" class="Symbol">((</a><a id="10496" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10496" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="10498" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10500" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10500" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="10503" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="10505" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10507" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10507" class="Bound">KA</a> <a id="10510" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="10512" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10512" class="Bound">B≅C</a><a id="10515" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="10518" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="10520" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3150" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a> <a id="10525" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10641" class="Function">sA</a> <a id="10528" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#10543" class="Function">B≤A</a>

Next we observe that lifting to a higher universe does not break the property of being a subalgebra of an algebra of a class.  In other words, if we lift a subalgebra of an algebra in a class, the result is still a subalgebra of an algebra in the class.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="12652" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12434" class="Function">lift-alg-subP</a> <a id="12666" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="12667" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12667" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="12668" class="Symbol">}(</a><a id="12670" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12670" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="12672" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12674" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12675" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12675" class="Bound">𝑪</a> <a id="12677" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12679" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12679" class="Bound">C≤A</a><a id="12682" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12684" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12686" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12686" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="12689" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#14564" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="12691" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#12691" class="Bound">B≅C</a> <a id="12695" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12697" class="Symbol">=</a>

The next lemma would be too obvious to care about were it not for the fact that we'll need it later, so it too must be formalized.

We need to formalize one more lemma before arriving the main objective of this section, which is the proof of the inclusion PS⊆SP.

 <a id="15460" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15460" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15462" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15464" href="Algebras.Products.html#908" class="Function">⨅</a> <a id="15466" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14910" class="Function">𝒜</a> <a id="15468" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="15470" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="15472" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14844" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
 <a id="15475" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15460" class="Function">ξ</a> <a id="15477" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="15479" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3918" class="InductiveConstructor">produ</a> <a id="15485" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="15488" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15488" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15490" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="15492" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#8903" class="Function">P-expa</a> <a id="15499" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15500" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13569" class="Function Operator">∣</a> <a id="15502" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13651" class="Function">snd</a> <a id="15506" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13647" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15508" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#14853" class="Bound">B≤K</a> <a id="15512" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15488" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="15514" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13647" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="15516" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13569" class="Function Operator">∣</a><a id="15517" class="Symbol">))</a>


</pre>



#### <a id="PS-in-SP">PS(𝒦) ⊆ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we are in a position to prove that a product of subalgebras of algebras in a class 𝒦 is a subalgebra of a product of algebras in 𝒦.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="15780" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="15787" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15788" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15788" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="15790" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="15792" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="15797" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="15798" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="15806" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15742" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="15808" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="15809" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="15811" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="15814" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15742" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="15815" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="15819" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="15826" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="15827" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="15828" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" <a id="16920" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15733" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16926" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16926" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16930" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16931" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4082" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a><a id="16936" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16937" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16937" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16938" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16940" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16940" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16941" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="16943" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16943" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="16946" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16946" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="16949" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16951" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="16953" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3291" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="16958" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16959" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15733" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16965" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16926" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16969" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16943" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="16971" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16973" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16946" class="Bound">A≅B</a>
<a id="16977" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15733" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="16983" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16983" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="16987" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16988" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4161" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a><a id="16993" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="16994" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16994" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="16995" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="16997" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16997" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="16998" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17000" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17000" class="Bound">pA</a> <a id="17003" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17003" class="Bound">A≅B</a><a id="17006" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17008" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17010" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3291" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17015" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17016" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#15733" class="Function">PS⊆SP</a> <a id="17022" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#16983" class="Bound">hfe</a> <a id="17026" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17000" class="Bound">pA</a><a id="17028" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17030" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17003" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>



#### <a id="more-class-inclusions">More class inclusions</a>

We conclude this subsection with three more inclusion relations that will have bit parts to play later (e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem).

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="P⊆V"></a><a id="17280" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17280" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17284" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17286" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17287" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17287" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17289" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17289" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="17291" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17293" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="17301" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17303" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17303" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17305" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17307" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17312" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17313" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17321" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17287" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17323" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17324" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17326" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17329" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17287" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17330" class="Symbol">)}</a> <a id="17333" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="17335" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17336" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17337" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17287" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17338" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17340" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17289" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17341" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17343" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17303" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17345" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="17347" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a><a id="17348" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17287" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17350" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17352" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17289" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17353" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17355" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17303" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="SP⊆V"></a><a id="17622" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17627" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17629" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17630" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17630" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17632" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17632" class="Bound">𝓦</a> <a id="17634" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17636" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="17644" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17646" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17646" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="17648" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="17650" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="17655" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17656" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="17664" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17630" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17666" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="17667" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="17669" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="17672" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17630" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17673" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="17677" class="Symbol">→</a>     <a id="17683" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="17684" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17685" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17630" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17687" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17689" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17632" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17690" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17692" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17630" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="17694" href="Agda.Primitive.html#636" class="Function Operator">⊔</a> <a id="17696" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17632" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17697" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17699" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17700" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="17701" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17702" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17630" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="17703" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17705" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17632" class="Bound">𝓦</a><a id="17706" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17708" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17646" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="17709" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17711" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="17713" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="17715" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17646" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

<a id="17718" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17723" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17724" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3030" class="InductiveConstructor">sbase</a><a id="17729" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17730" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17730" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17731" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17733" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17733" class="Bound">PCloA</a><a id="17738" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17740" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17742" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17280" class="Function">P⊆V</a> <a id="17746" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17747" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4161" class="InductiveConstructor">pisow</a> <a id="17753" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17733" class="Bound">PCloA</a> <a id="17759" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4959" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="17769" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17771" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17776" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17777" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3086" class="InductiveConstructor">slift</a><a id="17782" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17783" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17783" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17784" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17786" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17786" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17787" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17789" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17791" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4780" class="InductiveConstructor">vliftw</a> <a id="17798" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17799" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17804" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17786" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17805" class="Symbol">)</a>
<a id="17807" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17812" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3150" class="InductiveConstructor">ssub</a><a id="17817" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17818" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17818" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17819" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17821" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17821" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17822" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17824" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17824" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="17828" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17828" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="17831" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17833" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17835" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5008" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="17842" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17843" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17848" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17824" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="17851" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17853" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17828" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="17857" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17862" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17863" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3228" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a><a id="17868" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="17869" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17869" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="17870" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="17872" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17872" class="Bound">𝑩</a><a id="17873" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="17875" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17875" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="17879" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17879" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="17882" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17884" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17886" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5008" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="17893" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17894" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17899" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17875" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="17902" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17904" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17879" class="Bound">B≤A</a>
<a id="17908" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17913" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17914" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3291" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="17919" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17919" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="17921" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17921" class="Bound">x₁</a><a id="17923" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17925" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="17927" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5313" class="InductiveConstructor">visow</a> <a id="17933" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="17934" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17622" class="Function">SP⊆V</a> <a id="17939" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17919" class="Bound">x</a><a id="17940" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="17942" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#17921" class="Bound">x₁</a>

</pre>

We just proved that `SP(𝒦) ⊆ V(𝒦)`, and we did so under fairly general assumptions about the universe level parameters.  Unfortunately, this is sometimes not quite general enough, so we now prove the inclusion again for the specific universe parameters that align with subsequent applications of this result.

<pre class="Agda">

 <a id="18337" class="Symbol">→</a>      <a id="18344" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a><a id="18345" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18346" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18349" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18291" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18350" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18352" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18355" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18291" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18357" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18358" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18360" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18361" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="18362" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18363" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18291" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18364" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="18366" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18369" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18291" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="18370" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="18372" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18305" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="18373" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18375" href="Relations.Unary.html#2280" class="Function Operator">⊆</a> <a id="18377" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4567" class="Datatype">V</a> <a id="18379" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18305" class="Bound">𝒦</a>

  <a id="18600" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18567" class="Function">B≤lA</a> <a id="18605" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18607" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18608" href="Subalgebras.Subalgebras.html#8206" class="Function">lift-alg-≤-lift</a> <a id="18624" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18515" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18626" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="18627" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18512" class="Bound">𝑨</a><a id="18628" class="Symbol">})</a> <a id="18631" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18522" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

<a id="18636" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18282" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18642" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18643" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3228" class="InductiveConstructor">ssubw</a> <a id="18649" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18649" class="Bound">spA</a> <a id="18653" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18653" class="Bound">B≤A</a><a id="18656" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18658" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18660" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#5008" class="InductiveConstructor">vssubw</a> <a id="18667" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18668" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18282" class="Function">SP⊆V&#39;</a> <a id="18674" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18649" class="Bound">spA</a><a id="18677" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18679" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18653" class="Bound">B≤A</a>

  <a id="18749" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18749" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18751" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="18753" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18762" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18702" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18764" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18765" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18768" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18691" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18770" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18771" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18773" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#1151" class="Function Operator">≅</a> <a id="18775" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18705" class="Bound">𝑩</a>
  <a id="18779" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18749" class="Function">γ</a> <a id="18781" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="18783" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4495" class="Function">Trans-≅</a> <a id="18791" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18792" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="18801" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18702" class="Bound">𝑨</a> <a id="18803" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18804" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="18807" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18691" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="18809" href="Agda.Primitive.html#606" class="Function Operator">⁺</a><a id="18810" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="18813" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18705" class="Bound">𝑩</a> <a id="18815" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="18816" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#2988" class="Function">sym-≅</a> <a id="18822" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4959" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a><a id="18832" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="18834" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#18710" class="Bound">A≅B</a>

</pre>


#### <a id="S-in-SP">⨅ S(𝒦) ∈ SP(𝒦)</a>

Finally, we prove a result that plays an important role, e.g., in the formal proof of Birkhoff's Theorem. As we saw in [Algebras.Products][], the (informal) product `⨅ S(𝒦)` of all subalgebras of algebras in 𝒦 is implemented (formally) in the [UALib][] as `⨅ 𝔄 S(𝒦)`. Our goal is to prove that this product belongs to `SP(𝒦)`. We do so by first proving that the product belongs to `PS(𝒦)` and then applying the `PS⊆SP` lemma.

<pre class="Agda">

<a id="class-prod-s-∈-ps"></a><a id="19334" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19334" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19352" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19354" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19355" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19355" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19357" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19359" href="Agda.Primitive.html#423" class="Function">Universe</a><a id="19367" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19369" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19369" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="19371" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19373" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19355" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19375" href="Universes.html#403" class="Function Operator">̇</a><a id="19376" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19378" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19378" class="Bound">𝒦</a> <a id="19380" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19382" href="Relations.Unary.html#959" class="Function">Pred</a> <a id="19387" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19388" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19396" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19355" class="Bound">𝓤</a> <a id="19398" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a><a id="19399" class="Symbol">)(</a><a id="19401" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19404" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19355" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19405" class="Symbol">)}</a>
 <a id="19409" class="Symbol">→</a>                  <a id="19428" href="Algebras.Products.html#3936" class="Function">class-product</a> <a id="19442" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19443" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19355" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19444" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19446" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19355" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19447" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19449" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19369" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19450" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19452" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19453" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19455" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19378" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19456" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19458" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19460" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19461" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a><a id="19462" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19463" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19466" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19355" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19467" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19469" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19472" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19355" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19473" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="19475" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19476" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19478" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19378" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19479" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="19483" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19334" class="Function">class-prod-s-∈-ps</a> <a id="19501" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="19502" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19503" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19505" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19505" class="Bound">X</a><a id="19506" class="Symbol">}{</a><a id="19508" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19508" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19509" class="Symbol">}</a>  <a id="19512" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19514" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#4082" class="InductiveConstructor">pisou</a> <a id="19520" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19788" class="Function">psPllA</a> <a id="19527" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19528" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#6804" class="Function">⨅≅</a> <a id="19531" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#545" class="Bound">gfe</a> <a id="19535" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19839" class="Function">llA≅A</a><a id="19540" class="Symbol">)</a>
 <a id="19543" class="Keyword">where</a>
  <a id="19551" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19551" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19554" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19554" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19558" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19560" href="Algebras.Products.html#2792" class="Function">ℑ</a> <a id="19562" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19563" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19565" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19508" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19566" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19568" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19570" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#694" class="Function">Algebra</a> <a id="19578" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19579" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19582" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19583" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19585" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#526" class="Bound">𝑆</a>
  <a id="19589" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19551" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19592" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19592" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19594" class="Symbol">=</a>  <a id="19597" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="19606" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19607" href="Algebras.Products.html#3737" class="Function">𝔄</a> <a id="19609" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19610" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19612" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19508" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19613" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19615" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19592" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19616" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19618" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19619" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19622" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19623" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="19627" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19554" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19631" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19631" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19633" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19635" href="Algebras.Algebras.html#4659" class="Function">lift-alg</a> <a id="19644" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19645" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19551" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19648" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19631" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19649" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19651" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19652" href="Algebras.Products.html#1918" class="Function">ov</a> <a id="19655" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19502" class="Bound">𝓤</a><a id="19656" class="Symbol">)</a>

  <a id="19661" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19661" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="19665" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19667" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19669" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19669" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19671" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19673" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19674" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19551" class="Function">lA</a> <a id="19677" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19669" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19678" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19680" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19682" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19684" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19508" class="Bound">𝒦</a>
  <a id="19688" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19661" class="Function">slA</a> <a id="19692" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19692" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19694" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="19696" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3291" class="InductiveConstructor">siso</a> <a id="19701" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19702" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13573" class="Function">fst</a> <a id="19706" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13647" class="Function Operator">∥</a> <a id="19708" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19692" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19710" href="Prelude.Preliminaries.html#13647" class="Function Operator">∥</a><a id="19711" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19713" href="Homomorphisms.Isomorphisms.html#4959" class="Function">lift-alg-≅</a>

  <a id="19727" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19727" class="Function">psllA</a> <a id="19733" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="19735" class="Symbol">∀</a> <a id="19737" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19737" class="Bound">i</a> <a id="19739" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="19741" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19742" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19554" class="Function">llA</a> <a id="19746" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19737" class="Bound">i</a><a id="19747" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="19749" href="Relations.Unary.html#1958" class="Function Operator">∈</a> <a id="19751" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#3628" class="Datatype">P</a> <a id="19753" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="19754" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#2939" class="Datatype">S</a> <a id="19756" href="Varieties.Varieties.html#19508" class="Bound">𝒦</a><a id="19757" class="Symbol">)</a>
